** helpful-mode-map



Key             Binding

TAB		forward-button
RET		helpful-visit-reference
SPC		scroll-up-command
-		negative-argument
1 .. 9		digit-argument
<		beginning-of-buffer
>		end-of-buffer
g		helpful-update
n		forward-button
p		backward-button
q		quit-window
DEL		scroll-down-command
S-SPC		scroll-down-command
<backtab>	backward-button

<normal-state> RET		helpful-visit-reference
<normal-state> q		quit-window
<normal-state> <backtab>	backward-button
<normal-state> <tab>		forward-button

<remap> <revert-buffer>		helpful-update
<remap> <revert-buffer-quick>	helpful-update

g r		revert-buffer

<normal-state> g ?	describe-mode
<normal-state> g O	push-button

  (this binding is currently shadowed)

<Bury buffer>			magit-mode-bury-buffer

<Show another buffer>		magit-display-repository-buffer

<     Bisect...>		magit-bisect
<     Branch...>		magit-branch
<     Cherries...>		magit-cherry
<     Clone...>			magit-clone
<     Commit...>		magit-commit
<     Diff...>			magit-diff
<     Ediff...>			magit-ediff
<     Fetch...>			magit-fetch
<     Ignore...>		magit-gitignore
<     Init...>			magit-init
<     Log...>			magit-log
<     Merge...>			magit-merge
<     Pull...>			magit-pull
<     Push...>			magit-push
<     Rebase...>		magit-rebase
<     References...>		magit-show-refs
<     Remote...>		magit-remote
<     Stash...>			magit-stash
<     Tag...>			magit-tag

<Advanced> <Apply patches...>	magit-am
<Advanced> <Format patches...>	magit-patch
<Advanced> <Note...>		magit-notes
<Advanced> <Run...>		magit-run
<Advanced> <Submodule...>	magit-submodule
<Advanced> <Subtree...>		magit-subtree
<Advanced> <Worktree...>	magit-worktree

<Change buffer arguments> <Log arguments>  magit-log-refresh
